    [SubmittedAt] datetime2 NOT NULL DEFAULT (CURRENT_TIMESTAMP),
    CONSTRAINT [PK_submissions] PRIMARY KEY ([Id]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_submissions_phases_PhaseId] FOREIGN KEY ([PhaseId]) REFERENCES [phases] ([Id]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_submissions_topic_versions_TopicVersionId] FOREIGN KEY ([TopicVersionId]) REFERENCES [topic_versions] ([Id]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_submissions_users_SubmittedBy] FOREIGN KEY ([SubmittedBy]) REFERENCES [users] ([Id]) ON DELETE CASCADE
);
